I recommend without reservation‚Ä¶<//review>

Amazing concert acoustics with beautiful views of the harbor and downtown.  Projections around the perimeter of the shell help tell stories in a subtle way without being a distraction.  Only wish seating was pitched a but more to allow for better viewing of the stage.  Turf is comfortable and spacious for extended shows.<//Text>

< Rating>
3</Rating>
< Review>
The three stars I am offering up are mainly for the construction crews who did a fantastic job throughout the project. These guys kicked hiney and I spent enough time very near their location to see them actually building this structure for several months. Diligent and professional as they could be and friendly as passer-byes with their inquisiting minds passed by. I'm looking forward to returning here to see something in person.

When they were installed the lighting system I remember thinking as I looked in that direction it seemed as if the sun rose and set in succession again and again at night as they programmed it to function like it was supposed to.  It was
very neat to see something like that coming to life.

My best wishes for this venue and it's upcoming events!  During this time or I should say phase of our health consciousness, it will do good to see something bring happiness and joy to those who visit and not to mention it's fantastic location on the bay.

~JR~<//Review>

< text>
Well,being a bit picky about quality donuts, I was pleasantly surprised that the glazed donuts were probably the best I've ever had. As well as the chocolate buttermilk.....however I'm a stickler for chocolate old fashioned donuts & I've had better,Manleys are good but I've had better. I had a sandwich there too & the priced are like 5-6 dollars. Totally reasonable & tastes descent, but it's the donuts that are the draw.  One thing you have to be ready for is its cash only. When you pull up there's only room for like 2 cars but don't worry, if you go into the parking lot which looks small from the front there's actually plenty of room in the back. It reams a very low key place to grab a quick sandwich on a lunch break & maybe bring some donuts back for your coworkers,lol.<//text>

<time>1605070818700< /time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
I literally woke up in the middle of the night thinking about dumplings and when I shared my quirky craving to my husband, he was quickly on board.
I searched for dumplings and Hao Bao popped up with rave reviews. Initially I saw the midtown location and was bummed they were only open for lunch but when I realized the Stockton Blvd location was open until 6:30pm I hustled out the door to pick up some dumplings!
We walked into a bright and super clean space and were greeted warmly.
Ordering was super easy and fast, and we had our food in hand in 10 minutes. In the car,  the lovely steamy smell of dumplings wafted into my nose and made my mouth water the entire trip.

Our dumplings were tender, moist, and super flavorful. We ordered the pork and beef dumplings (boiled) as well as the house noodles. Everything averaged under $10 and it was so much food we have leftovers for days.

They are very satisfying and affordable and remind me of dumpling houses in SF and Asia.
So if you‚Äôre looking for dumplings that are filling and tasty, I recommend Hao Bao!< /Review>

I love this place! Clean, modern facilities,  and the wait is never long to order or get food. Staff is very friendly and helpful. The prices are very low. I'm sensitive to the food I eat. Came here for lunch today. I just wanted dumplings...

I was greeted as i walked in..  because of covid it is take out or delivery only. They do however have tables outside to sit and eat.

They offer veggie...chicken...beef and pork dumplings...starting at 4.99 for 8 and 7.99 for 16 of one flavor.

House made noodles. 8.99
dumpling soup 8.49 or 8.99..thai tea...ect.

They offer to cook them 3 ways boiled...pan fried or deep fried.

They also have different sauces...teriyaki sauce...sesame or house which is kind of like spicy goyza sauce...they are all so good...

I ordered 16 pork dumplings to eat for lunch. I had them pan fried. 7.99.

I loved them so much...that i then ordered 50 frozen dumplings to take home with all 3 sauces.

I have not tried anything else here...but based on these alone...i would come back. Just wonderful.

If you are looking for catering...frozen dumplings to take home or just a few for lunch...you will not regret eating hereüòÄüòÄüòÄüòÄ< /text>

<user_id>107388689091175516628</user_id><Pics>None</Pics>< Review>
It's funny how things go sometimes...I was looking to get a bahn mi at Duk Huong but had my dog and didn't want to leave him in the car. While I was trying to figure out where to leave him while I went inside, I noticed the new Hao Bao across the way with outside seating! Alright, I can have dumplings...and glad I did! This is a cool little place that keeps it basic with dumplings and a soup with dumplings. Dumplings come with your choice of beef, pork, chicken or veggie, 8 or 16 pieces. Then you choose if you want boiled, pan fried or deep fried. They have 3 sauces to choose, house (sweeter with chilli's), sesame or teriyaki. I got the beef boiled and an order of veggie pan fried. They were really good! Decent amount of flavorful filling.  13 pieces were enough for me (my dog ate 3). 2 thumbs up from me and 2 paws up from Darwin.
We will definitely return!<//Review>

<UserId.>107922827130364598361</UserId.><username>Jim J<//username><time>1547329496516< /time><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
TLDR: Excellent prices, excellent service, professional work. This is the place to go for any tire related anything, and is now my personal go-to for tires that I would recommend to everyone.

Full review:

I have been to several tire places and this one is the best of the lot without question.

I called ahead to make sure they had what I needed, as the vehicle in question has uncommon tires. There was a short wait while stock was confirmed, and was subsequently pleasantly suprised to hear the not only did they have 4 tires of the correct size, but they were able to undercut their competitions price.

There is no reduction of quality of service and work from the lower price, which is a definite win in my book. It did take longer than one might expect, but that was due to my tires being really wide as well as run-flat tires, which adds a significant degree of difficulty (have done tires myself in the past with a manual tire machine, so have a bit of experience in this area). Despite the difficulty,  the work was done with no complaints and the team of two brothers worked together very well to complete the job to perfection. They realised that the work was taking a while without me saying anything, and proceeded to explain exactly what was going on without any prompting at all, which shows their professionalism and knowledge in action.

After all was said and done, I was told to bring my car right back if there were any issues and they would take care of it. These guys rock!

2 Months Later: As happy now as on day 1; my truck needs tires soon and I know exactly who to call!

7 Months Later: Awesomely epic service, 'nuff said</Review>

<rate>1< /rate>< review>
$5 minimum for credit cards.

This location no longer serve item selection combos, a la carte only. Pricing is also high for Chinese food standard, $9-10 for a one item combo.

They do not clean their soda machine properly. The soda I was served tastes like cleaning solution and bleach.

The portion is small for the pricing.

The food definitely uses less oil and grease when compared to other Chinese food location, but the flavoring is extremely bland. Everything tastes like water-downed soy sauce. A lot of the natural ingredients are not seasoned properly and have no flavor or just tastes like soy sauce.

For the price you are paying, you are much better off selecting the other Chinese food locations within the area.< /review>

< review>
I just want to begin by saying that this business definitely deserves all the five star ratings.  I asked the owner of this company to cater my father's 75th surprise birthday party two weekends ago.  I had spent many hours online searching nearby locations for good quality caterers and found that they are very hard to come by.  I live in Arizona and was trying to plan his party from a state away.  Parties are already hard to plan, but they are even harder to plan when you are doing it from a different state.

Lets start off with the fact that I picked this company only based off of their reviews and Sean's amazing communication.  Sean called me almost immediately after I sent my email (which I found is rare in this business lately).  Throughout the entire process leading up to the event, he was super easy to get in touch with by phone and email.  He responded to my emails within a day and made the process of making changes to our menu or party size very easy. He was very kind, easy to work with, and understanding.

I usually would taste test food before booking a caterer, but given that I lived so far away, I didn't really have that option.  I was really nervous about hiring a company I had never heard of or tried myself.  However,  I read the reviews, talked my plans over with Sean, and quickly took a leap of faith.  I can't tell you how relieved I was to have this company take over the responsibility of preparing a meal for 60 people.  They definitely did not disappoint.  All the guests were so impressed and said it was the best BBQ food they had ever had.

My brother also called me recently and expressed that guests are still raving about the food two weeks later.  He said that guests keep asking him where we found the caterer and how they can get in touch with him. My father LOVED the food and was so impressed that BBQ catering could be so high quality and tasty.

Most importantly, the food was amazing.  It was very flavorful, the meats were juicy (not dried out), freshly made, and plentiful.  We never ran out of food and people were returning for seconds.  There are many selections of food to choose from and there are even options for vegetarians which you don't really think about in regards to a BBQ.  We chose the ribs, chicken, tri tip, chipotle mac and cheese, fresh green salad, deviled potato salad, mixed grilled veggies, dinner rolls.  I would hire them again in a heartbeat and even have considered one day using them for my wedding!

THANK YOU SEAN and CV BBQ for coming all the way out to help make my Dad's surprise party such a huge success.  He loved it!! You were all so kind and professional, and the food really was impressive.  You have a great business, and I hope you will still be around for future events!!!

Taylor</review>

< Review>
It seems that weddings are defined--for better or worse, for richer or poorer--by their food. In that regard, CV BBQ helped make my wedding a success.

Pretty early on my now-wife and I decided that our wedding had to be nice but not fussy. Like a backyard dinner party but elevated. She being from Santa Barbara, tri-tip was one of the early options for the dinner menu. After finding CV BBQ here on Yelp we quickly made contact with Sean, who was responsive and friendly from start to finish. (This, I came to realize, is a rare thing in the wedding planning world.) Suffice it to say that our mid-week trip to Palm Springs for a tasting was well worth it and we booked Sean's company without ever trying another caterer. It was affordable, fit our criteria, and most importantly delicious.

Tri-tip, chicken, mac and cheese, potato salad, kale Caesar salad (a slight modification to their normal Caesar salad) and grilled mixed vegetables: ordered!

Come wedding day, the smell of grilled meats were wafting across the venue and I'd like to think that it made the whole ceremony all that more enjoyable. And as I stood ready to gorge myself on food I heard someone yell, "Congratulations, David!" It was Sean of CV BBQ, standing in the middle of the service line alongside his employees. Now, it's hard to make well-rounded judgments on a person through such few interactions but when you see the boss standing alongside his people, that's saying a whole hell of a lot. Not only about the pride he has in his company but also in his staff and in his food.

But enough about all that. How was the food?! The tri-tip was obviously the star. Cooked medium and sliced thin, there was no more left by the end of the night. I wish I'd had more of it looking back but I was so nervous about the first dance that I didn't want to over-stuff myself and get sick all over the dance floor. The chicken, unlike most others, was exceedingly moist probably because they use dark meat instead of over-hyped white meat. Sean and his staff used baby kale for the Caesar and it was probably much more enjoyable for everyone when compared to the tougher adult kale. But I think what I was most impressed by were the vegetables considering vegetables and vegetarian options are often overlooked at wedding meals. These were smoky, still firm and even included pineapple to help add acid and flavor.

I cannot stress enough how helpful and kind CV BBQ was during our whole ceremony. People kept coming up to me to say how nice the catering staff and bartenders (hired through CV BBQ) were. Of course, it was quickly followed up with something to the effect of "...and the food was SO GOOD!"

Thank you, Sean and company, for making our day special and delicious.< /Review>

<Pictures>None</Pictures>< Text>
If you're thinking of serving traditional cold chicken and sad iceberg salads at your wedding...don't. CV BBQ was such a wonderful highlight for our intimate wedding in Yucca Valley late February. We were planning from Michigan and the process couldn't have been easier.

We thought we wanted a family style dinner, but the cost of other vendors we researched was so steep for a group of 20 and the response times were usually lacking. From my first email with Sean he was so responsive and helpful. We knew we all love a good BBQ and heard CV BBQ brought an elevated experience, so we had no concerns with booking without a tasting.

On our wedding day the scent of tri-tip, ribs, and grilled chicken wafting over the property was incredible. The staff was so friendly and the food stayed hot! I wasn't sure what to expect for the buffet table, but the presentation looked great.

THE FOOD
Let's just say I'm glad my dress was stretchy. I think I ate no less than 10 ribs and a pile of tri-tip. We subbed kale for the lettuce in the caesar salad and I loved it because I felt like I was at least eating some vegetables. (I was just trying to stay warm with meat sweats tbh). The mashed potatoes were creamy and amazing.

Our friends and family LOVED the food as much as we did. We still hear about it. My mouth is watering thinking about it. Imagine a tasty backyard BBQ memory then imagine if it was even better - that's CV BBQ.

We realized afterward that the team didn't get their gratuity so we sent it along a couple of weeks ago (so sorry!) If you're planning a no-fuss, destination wedding or just want really really good food...book them! Thank you so much Sean and team for an incredible wedding dinner.< /Text>

<review>We had the pleasure of having CV BBQ cater our wedding 2 weeks ago in Palm Springs. Everyone at our wedding told us repeatedly how DELICIOUS the food was. Most people went for seconds, and that's how you know they are genuinely impressed. It was buffet style but Sean, the owner, personally plated the bride and groom's plates with loads of deliciousness. His staffs and bartenders are friendly and professional as well. We could not have been happier with the food and service.

Let's be honest, most guests don't remember the food of weddings because they are usually blend, mediocre and not filling. We had the option of choosing one of the caterers that provided fancy dishes and Hors d'oeuvres we couldn't pronounce, but we are so glad to have gone with CV BBQ. They use top notch ingredients to produce unpretentious and simply delicious food.

If you're considering between CV BBQ or another standard plated course meal place, look no further, go with CV BBQ! And be sure to order more of the ribs than you think people will want, because they will want more! The tri-tip (they slice in front of you) and chicken were divine as well, but everyone wanted more of the ribs for seconds so we ran out of them. The mac-n-cheese, mushrooms and mashed potatoes compliment the meats so well and are great options for vegetarian guests.

Sean is the most personable and solution-oriented person to work with. Every wedding will run through challenges. The entire time I felt like I had Sean's full support and commitment to solve problems together. He was flexible enough to work around my venue's restrictions and my last minute change of services without complaining. Everything went without a hitch in our eyes. Both my husband and I applaud his work ethic.

Last but not least, Sean allows you to bring your own liquor as a lot of caterers would rather charge you the premium on alcohol. We were able to rent 2 bartenders from CV BBQ and all the staff members to pass around appetizers and pour water and wine during the dinner. On top of Sean's very reasonable price for food, it saved us a lot of money to bring our own drinks.

You are in for a serious treat if you go with CV BBQ! Good luck!< /review>< name>
Laycee Berkas</name>

< review>
If you are looking for juicy, light, crispy, tender, flavorful fried chicken that packs a great heat, you have come to the right place! Main Chick has one of the best fried chickens in this area, and I am pleasantly surprised by my order. It has all the greatness of traditional fried chicken, but minus the excessive fat. The chicken is perfect, and spice level 4 is THE match for me (be ware, it's really hot). The seasoning on the fries is right on point, and the house sauce is perfect for the chicken and the fries.
My only suggestion is that the slider bun and the slaw is a bit underwhelming, with such a flavor packed chicken you need a stronger slaw, either in sourness or texture.< /review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
I saw an article about Main Chick opening up a location down here and had to come by. Never been to one before but friends had mentioned them being amazing up in Pasadena. All I can say is...More Please!!

I got the Combo #1 which comes with 1 chicken strip with a pickle slice on top, 1 chicken sandwich a small container of MC sauce and fries. They give about 5 options I believe for spice level and I'm a bit of a spice wimp so I chose mild and thank heavens I did as even their mild is on the hot side for my taste but delicious nonetheless.
My order came by quickly, only bout 5 min or so wait time and the lady at the register opened the box up to show everything was in there which, considering everything is to go right now, was a nice customer service touch.
I tried the fries first, which were nice and thick with just enough seasoning. The MC sauce really gave them an extra kick though; truly a delicious unique flavor. The chicken strip had a ton of dry rub seasoning on it which I love but was also nice hot and juicy on the inside, so good! I then tried the sandwich and devoured that in 3 or 4 bites, enough said haha.
If I could give one critique I'd say the cardboard box it came in had a lot of likely grease stains on it, not the most pleasant thing to see but that was it.
Great customer service, great taste, will definitely be back again.</Text>

< Text>
By far the best chicken sandwich I‚Äôve had that lives up to their spice level and flavor.

Recommend to call in your orders ahead of time. We waited until we got there and it was a good 20-30 minutes when she told us 10-15 minutes. There were a lot of phone orders and people coming in to pickup.

Their menu is so simple with five combo choices and a few a la carte choices. Made it so easy to order.

We got combo #3 which was two chicken sandwiches with crinkle cut fries for $15. We got one sandwich mild and the other spicy. We also got one leg quarter $4.50 in medium spice. It all came with Main Chick sauce.

The orders was packed neatly in boxes. When I got home, I opened the leg quarter first and immediately, the medium spice aroma ticketed my nose. That‚Äôs how strong it was.

I took a bite of the sandwich and it had the crispy crunchy texture and juicy chicken with all the amazing flavors and perfect amount of spice level. Mild had a slight kick and I could handle medium while spicy would be too much for me.

Due to COVID19, it‚Äôs only take out and no dining in or outdoor. Not that much space so only one at a time inside at the counter.

Plenty of parking spaces in this plaza. Located next to the theater and Indian restaurant.<//Text>

<Review>Main Chick Hot Chicken has been open for about a week, so I had to try out this new chicken spot. I ordered combo #2. It has 2 chicken sandwiches and crinkle fries. As far as the spice level, I chose the Spicy level of heat. The hottest level is called Supreme, and it requires a waiver before consuming that one. I would have liked to sample the Supreme before I ordered my food, but the young lady said that it was not possible. I‚Äôve been able to sample sauces at other chicken restaurants, but maybe covid 19 policies has something to do with it. The seasoning of the chicken was spot on. In addition, I would say that the customer service was great. The people that worked there were friendly and helpful. The price point seems to be a bit higher than most places for similar portioned and quality chicken. <review>This is my family's go to Mexican restaurant. I've had many different items off the menu. I've never had a bad meal here. Staff is always quick and friendly. Plenty of chips and salsa when you arrive. Salsa has a nice zing to it. Drink orders are taken quickly. Orders arrive in a timely manner. Always plenty to eat or even take home.

Urbano's is a clean, typically decorated Mexican restaurant. Spacious, never over crowded, with a nice full bar and plenty of TV's playing sports. Also an outside dining area.

This trip my guest had the 2 burritos combination plate. I opted for my favorite, a special on this night, Pozole. If you never have had it it's like a salsa soup with big chunks of slow cooked pork or chicken in it. Yum.

Urbano's servers it with fresh cabbage, cilantro, lemon wedge, and a bowl of dried oregano. Add the ingredients, give the lemon squeeze, sprinkle the oregano, and bring your taste buds alive. It's a 5 star bowl of soup.l</review>< rate>

<Text>Food:
Their fried chicken is their signature food. The ribs are also delicious! The Cole slaw is gross. The macaroni salad is okay. The corn bread is good. Could be a little bit sweeter. Make sure you bring your own water.

Service:
Service is okay. They hand you their food. They keep the area pretty clean. The food is delivered from the front building to the back.

Seating:
Lots of benches, but the place can get very pack. There is grass for picnic if you choose to sit on the ground.

Only 1 restroom, which is always a wait here. <text>Some of the best fried chicken I've had. I had the opportunity to try this when a friend hosted their wedding reception here. (I know. What a freaking treat.) Best. Wedding Food. Ever. It's so yummy that I ask to come up here multiple times throughout the year. I'm not much a drinker so when I ask the husband to come up here, I offer to be DD as long as I get to stop here for some fried chicken and cornbread.

The backyard (literally) is a very casual place to grab lunch with some friends on a warm day. This past weekend when we went they had TEMPORARILY relocated to a vacant building down the street so they could accommodate guests during the colder months. GENIUS.

I haven't been to any fried chicken mecca but this place has some of the best fried chicken. The skin is crispy and flavorful but not overpowering. The chicken is juicy and tender. It's deliciousness. It's a little on the pricey-er side so prepare to shell out as you'll want to try everything.

This past weekend they had a lobster roll that we decided to try and it was good. It's expensive but it tasted good. The price point is like the crab sandwich at AT&T park but significantly tastes better.

If you don't have a reservation anywhere in Yountville and looking for something a little low-key - I highly recommend this spot.

The Pro-Tip if you know your schedule - order ahead online, especially if it's a warm busy weekend.</text><Rate>5</Rate></record>

<name>Walter Macalma< /name><date>1445993404310</date><rating>3</rating><Text>Thomas Keller, the Kingpin of Yountville‚Äôs version of a food truck this fast food shack has no inkling of Americana, Fine Dining. It‚Äôs an entire fast food joint built upon his signature dish. ‚ÄúButtermilk Fried Chicken‚Äù. You could order in person and wait an hour or order online and it will be ready somewhere between 30 and 40 minutes from ordering. Walk me down from the wine country oh modern man.

Oh golden delicious battered and deep fried chicken you are so moist and crunchy. It was strange to see they offering buckets a la KFC/Popeyes style. If you took Willie Mae‚Äôs and combined with Hatti B‚Äôs spice this is what you get.

Somewhere selling Fried chicken, ribs, cornbread, cookies and changing sides is pretty much southern BBQ, not something loosely connected in ownership to FL. This review is easy.

The chicken is still very good, but due to bulk and since it‚Äôs fast food you lose a little something in the quality because lets face it even if you eat out the box as you walk to the benches it‚Äôs nothing like getting it plated and garnished just for you. Here there is a dozen people‚Äôs orders in behind you, straight up assembly line style.

Seeing the menu you would think someone in the staff has a grandmother from the south that could have shown them how to properly make cornbread. It‚Äôs dry, lacking sweetness of fresh corn, it‚Äôs small. Regardless of the sides that 1 piece and 2 more sides is not worth it. Honestly you should just get the chicken. It‚Äôs a catastrophy with the side dishes, again as if 3 people each made 1 side and the portions were laughable. I myself, or someone I know beats each of his side dishes every day of the week and twice on Sunday. I take it back that this is southern BBQ anywhere else, nope this is an insult to BBQ side dishes. It makes sense when your waiting hours for to smoke your meats low and slow, why not perfect the side dishes here. Ice tea was basic. Potato salad had no zing, cole slaw had no contrast. You should have never tried to make pulled pork, now your really getting into that BBQ realm which puts a whole new category of criticism going up against my specialty palate, but I‚Äôll take it easy on that. low and slow or don't do it at all, do the pig some justice will ya. The cookie was about 250% overpriced.

The service is chaotic, but the scenery is nice, seeing as it‚Äôs not a restaurant and just a shack. I thought that Ad Hoc gave Thomas Keller and FL a bad name, but Addendum give ad hoc a bad name. This guy is hitching himself to the wrong horse post FL. Nominal value seeing as a large bucket cost near $50 and

To be fair the chicken beats most fried chicken on the west coast. Thomas Keller you went from Michelin master to jack of all trades master of none.<//Text>< pictures>

<review>Kitchen Mouse is a vegetarian restaurant on 59th avenue and Fig. Atmosphere is welcoming and relaxing. Interior decor resembles your own kitchen house with accented lights and classic dinner tables/chairs. Similarly, it is well organized, neat and lots of natural light. Outdoor seats are available albeit very limited. Prices are a bit on the high end for HP neighborhood. They accept cash and credit/debit card. Staff are friendly and professional. On a busy day, service can be slow and long lines. You need to order first before you take a table. We ordered their three stacks House Pancakes, made of oat, buckwheat, and corn flour with blue berries/strawberries, toasted coconut and maple syrup; and two scrambled eggs. Pancakes were flavorful and fluffy and thick; the eggs are perfectly cooked and their coffee was just good. Overall, if you like veggie breakfast KM is the place to be.< /review>< gmapID>

< Review>
The cute, retro kitschy decor is only the beginning at Kitchen Mouse. Catering to the vegan gluten-free crowd, the breakfast tacos can be made with either egg or tofu. I'm neither, so I chose the egg option and added the optional avocado. It was really good. Fresh corn tortillas filled with scrambled egg, lettuce and greens and drizzled with delicious creamy sauce.  I also opted for a strawberry corn muffin that was also delicious. My friend ordered the Sunshine Bowl which had seasonal fruit nestled on top of fresh homemade yogurt  and sprinkled with granola. Garnished with chia seeds and an edible flower, she said it was refreshing. She also had a gluten-free chocolate donut that she said was really good.  They offer bottomless coffee and free wifi as well. Definitely recommend Kitchen Mouse.</Review>

<user>102761999783078995895<//user>< Text>
HP is on its way to gentrification and Kitchen Mouse is part of this transformation.  Missing a couple of stars NOT because of the food.

Very long line, long wait, would have been nice to have been greeted and informed as it's not clear that you need to wait in line first to order before sitting down. You can't see the sign letting you know this because the sign is at the bottom of the counter and people are standing in front of it.  I thought people standing in line  were ordering to go.

After you order, it's all self service after that.  You need to get your own water, coffee, condiments.  They serve you your food and no one ever comes back to check on you.  Not sure that is the norm or if they're under staffed.

Very cute hipster space, but not a place for strollers.

Now that I know the rules of play, the food was good enough for me to go back and I'll give it another try.</Text>

<Name>Marissa Berrini<//Name><Date>1576978572154</Date><rating>5<//rating><Text>This is one of my favorite places in Los Angeles. Located in Highland Park, it's the perfect breakfast place for vegans and vegetarians. Even my husband who isn't vegan enjoys this restaurant. There are plenty of delicious options but my favorites are chilaquiles and a side order of snickerdoodle pancakes. It's heaven on Earth! The snickerdoodle pancakes come with the most amazing coconut whipped butter I've ever had. In terms of drinks I really love their lattes with almond milk and iced tea. Sometimes they gift mini cornbread muffins during their brunch service. If you have kids there's a play area in the back to keep them entertained. If you like to eat solo there's a wrap-around bar perfect for dining alone and people watching. Last but not least be sure to get there early because on the weekends there is normally a line. It's also great cuz you can order at the counter and not have to deal with splitting any checks when going with groups. <Pics>None<//Pics><text>Excellent vegetarian and vegan cuisine with a hometown country kitchen hippie vibe. I'm by no means a vegetarian, but this is a great place to stop for lunch or breakfast, especially with my friends who have more selective diets. Kitchen Mouse does have eggs for those of us who aren't vegetarian and the Stumptown drip coffee is self-serve and pretty darn good, or espresso and coldbrew if that's your jam.

They've got rice and veggie bowls, tacos, and standard breakfast fare like eggs, toast, and pancakes, or varieties of salads if you're looking for lunch fare.  I most recently had the weekend special, the jackfruit crab benedict. It's different, much lighter than a normal benedict, I don't think it had any bread, just eggs, seasoned jackfruit, and hollandaise on a bed of citrusy arugula. It was delicious, but could have used a bit more seasoning and I wish it came with toast as it wasn't terribly filling.

The line get pretty long on the weekends and seating can be hard to find, best to get here early if you want to beat the brunch rush. You order at the counter, paper menus can be found near the register. They'll give you a number to place on your table.<//text>< Resp>

< review>
ALWAYS NOISY.  Have had a hilarious time or two trying to order at the order-counter-register; wait-person and I could not hear each other over the bad music. You have to ratchet down expectations and assume loud group conversations, crying kids, random high pitched electronic messaging to the kitchen, trying to be drowned out with the bland music. I know, I know, I'm not in a library setting, I realize. (Though, they do have a fair collection of diverse cookbooks for your reading pleasure.) During a recent (usually) short wait for food, I downloaded a Decibel measuring smartphone app.  Just as I thought, 65 to 80 db, which the app says ranges /compares normal conversation at 3 feet to vacuum cleaner and alarm clocks (next level is power mower.) Evidence enough that this not just a figment of my imagination or misanthropic view. (Although....)
I usually order the GLK breakfast, or Avocado TLT or the whachacallit open-faced sandwich with sauerkraut on top. The rest makes me squeamish.
The vegan faux-Mexican dish my lunch-date ordered was a failure, obviously needing some visual help. It looked particularly disgusting. Doesn't culinary training encompass serving the food in an appearance that is appetizing and tasty?  Frequently notice the over use of salt here, especially in salads, even when requested not to add it. You'd think a health-concern such as this would be intuitive.  Hipsters sometimes are not so hip, I guess.< /review>
